[30;1m48 | [0m[35m* Cooperation with static type checking infrastructure â€“Â the API provides as much static type safety[0m
[30;1m49 | [0m[35m  as possible and only breaks it where there's no other option. For example the[0m
[30;1m50 | [0m[35m  [Injector.get](https://injector.readthedocs.io/en/latest/api.html#injector.Injector.get) method[0m
[30;1m51 | [0m[35m  is typed such that `injector.get(SomeType)` is statically declared to return an instance of[0m
[30;1m52 | [0m[35m  `SomeType`, therefore making it possible for tools such as [mypy](https://github.com/python/mypy) [0m
[30;1m53 | [0m[35m  type-check correctly the code using it.[0m
[30;1m54 | [0m[35m  [0m

[30;1m97 | [0m[35m   provides as much static type safety as possible and only breaks it[0m
[30;1m98 | [0m[35m   where thereâ€™s no other option. For example the[0m
[30;1m99 | [0m[35m   `Injector.get <https://injector.readthedocs.io/en/latest/api.html#injector.Injector.get>`__[0m
[30;1m100 | [0m[35m   method is typed such that ``injector.get(SomeType)`` is statically[0m
[30;1m101 | [0m[35m   declared to return an instance of ``SomeType``, therefore making it[0m
[30;1m102 | [0m[35m   possible for tools such as `mypy <https://github.com/python/mypy>`__[0m
[30;1m103 | [0m[35m   to type-check correctly the code using it.[0m
